<th>Misc. Notes
</th>
<td>As will be seen by comparing Fantasias No.2, 1st Dozen, and Nos.11 &amp; 12, 2nd Dozen (=Nos.23-24), some plates for the later impression have been entirely re-engraved, no doubt due to faults with the temperamental copper plates used (cracks in the plates are clearly visible on several pages).
